name:Mâ€aâ€nâ€mâ€aâ€nâ€kâ€eâ€nâ€aâ€lâ€iâ€uâ€dâ€a

posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:A group of five people booked the Crowne Plaza Hotel during the May Day holiday. More than a dozen people gave unanimous praise. No wonder this hotel has good reviews online, because it is indeed good. The reasons are as follows:
1. Superior twin room, the room is quite large, a family of four with twin beds and super large beds is very spacious.
2. As a relatively newly opened hotel (five-star for three years), all kinds of facilities are very new, the hotel environment is good, and the sanitary conditions are good.
There are rich parent-child facilities and a free children's playground (this is really great, the parents' hands are freed on vacation, the children play in the playground for two hours, and the parents play for two hours at the door, cool!)
Next to the playground is a swimming pool, and several children also had a lot of fun.
3. The geographical location is superior. Dongying is only suitable for self-driving. The hotel has many parking spaces. It only takes 5 minutes to go to the old village chief's lumpy soup.
4. The most important thing is that the service is good and the customer experience is good. For example, a family of four (children 7 and 9) does not need to pay extra for breakfast for a 1.5-meter child. The breakfast is rich and the breakfast is willing to extend the service time appropriately for customers. If the children do not eat much breakfast, they can pack a small portion and provide a packing box. We adults want to play mahjong in the evening (bring your own), and find a coffee table and chair in the hotel lobby that does not affect others. The hotel is very proactive in arranging it. It can be said that it meets all needs. At least it is not like many other hotels I have stayed in, where customers cannot do this or that when they have needs. Questions and Answers ? 
In short, I have stayed in many hotels, and the hardware and service of this hotel really exceeded my expectations (five-star hotels are very cost-effective). I booked it about a month ago, and it was more than 500 yuan including breakfast for two. Later, I looked at it and found that there were no notes when the room was booked. The remaining notes were more than 1,000 yuan per room, so if you have travel plans, it is recommended to book early and you can cancel it for free.
